These part\\n60:  * files contain the actual output data.\\n61:  *\\n62:  * <p>The sink uses a {@link BucketAssigner} to determine in which bucket directory each element\\n63:  * should be written to inside the base directory. The default {@code\\n65:  * BucketAssigner} is a {@link DateTimeBucketAssigner} which will create one new bucket every hour.\\n66:  * You can specify a custom {@code BucketAssigner} using the {@code\\n67:  * setBucketAssigner(bucketAssigner)} method, after calling {@link\\n68:  * StreamingFileSink#forRowFormat(Path, Encoder)} or {@link StreamingFileSink#forBulkFormat(Path,\\n69:  * BulkWriter.Factory)}.\\n70:  *\\n71:  * <p>The names of the part files could be defined using {@link OutputFileConfig}. This\\n72:  * configuration contains a part prefix and a part suffix that will be used with the parallel\\n73:  * subtask index of the sink and a rolling counter to determine the file names. For example with a\\n74:  * prefix \\\"prefix\\\" and a suffix \\\".ext\\\", a file named {@code \\\"prefix-1-17.ext\\\"} contains the data\\n75:  * from {@code subtask 1} of the sink and is the {@code 17th} bucket created by that subtask.\\n76:  *\\n77:  * <p>Part files roll based on the user-specified {@link RollingPolicy}. By default, a {@link\\n78:  * DefaultRollingPolicy} is used for row-encoded sink output; a {@link OnCheckpointRollingPolicy} is\\n79:  * used for bulk-encoded sink output.\\n80:  *\\n81:  * <p>In some scenarios, the open buckets are required to change based on time. In these cases, the\\n82:  * user can specify a {@code bucketCheckInterval} (by default 1m) and the sink will check\\n83:  * periodically and roll the part file if the specified rolling policy says so.\\n84:  *\\n85:  * <p>Part files can be in one of three states: {@code in-progress}, {@code pending} or {@code\\n86:  * finished}. The reason for this is how the sink works together with the checkpointing mechanism to\\n87:  * provide exactly-once semantics and fault-tolerance. The part file that is currently being written\\n88:  * to is {@code in-progress}. Once a part file is closed for writing it becomes {@code pending}.\\n89:  * When a checkpoint is successful the currently pending files will be moved to {@code finished}.\\n90:  *\\n91:  * <p>If case of a failure, and in order to guarantee exactly-once semantics, the sink should roll\\n92:  * back to the state it had when that last successful checkpoint occurred. To this end, when\\n93:  * restoring, the restored files in {@code pending} state are transferred into the {@code finished}\\n94:  * state while any {@code in-progress} files are rolled back, so that they do not contain data that\\n95:  * arrived after the checkpoint from which we restore.\\n96:  *\\n97:  * @param <IN> Type of the elements emitted by this sink\\n98:  * @deprecated Use {@link org.apache.flink.connector.file.sink.FileSink} instead.\\n99:  */\\n100: @Internal\\n101: public class StreamingFileSink<IN> extends RichSinkFunction<IN>\\n102:         implements CheckpointedFunction, CheckpointListener {\\n103: \\n104:     private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\\n105: \\n106:     // ------------------------ configuration fields --------------------------\\n107: \\n108:     private final long bucketCheckInterval;\\n109: \\n110:     private final BucketsBuilder<IN, ?, ? extends BucketsBuilder<IN, ?, ?>> bucketsBuilder;\\n111: \\n112:     // --------------------------- runtime fields -----------------------------\\n113: \\n114:     private transient StreamingFileSinkHelper<IN> helper;\\n115: \\n116:     /**\\n117:      * Creates a new {@code StreamingFileSink} that writes files to the given base directory with\\n118:      * the give buckets properties.\\n119:      */\\n120:     @VisibleForTesting\\n121: \",\"url\":\"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc@de39c3e1777c43fe3363b3fd7784bf46b57a99c2/-/blob/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/functions/sink/filesystem/legacy/StreamingFileSink.java%3FL1-120\"}"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"cce8ca2f-1f89-47a5-976c-06f667960df2","uuid":"d11bd4e4-98f8-4003-bdc8-322064f976e5","tool_use_result":{"content":"{\"content\":\"1: /*\\n2:  * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one\\n3:  * or more contributor license agreements. \n50: import java.io.IOException;\n51: import java.io.Serializable;\n52: \n53: /**\n54:  * Sink that emits its input elements to {@link FileSystem} files within buckets. This is integrated\n55:  * with the checkpointing mechanism to provide exactly once semantics.\n56:  *\n57:  * <p>When creating the sink a {@code basePath} must be specified. The base directory contains one\n58:  * directory for every bucket. The bucket directories themselves contain several part files, with at\n59:  * least one for each parallel subtask of the sink which is writing data to that bucket. These part\n60:  * files contain the actual output data.\n61:  *\n62:  * <p>The sink uses a {@link BucketAssigner} to determine in which bucket directory each element\n63:  * should be written to inside the base directory. The {@code BucketAssigner} can, for example, use\n64:  * time or a property of the element to determine the bucket directory. The default {@code\n65:  * BucketAssigner} is a {@link DateTimeBucketAssigner} which will create one new bucket every hour.\n66:  * You can specify a custom {@code BucketAssigner} using the {@code\n67:  * setBucketAssigner(bucketAssigner)} method, after calling {@link\n68:  * StreamingFileSink#forRowFormat(Path, Encoder)} or {@link StreamingFileSink#forBulkFormat(Path,\n69:  * BulkWriter.Factory)}.\n70:  *\n71:  * <p>The names of the part files could be defined using {@link OutputFileConfig}. This\n72:  * configuration contains a part prefix and a part suffix that will be used with the parallel\n73:  * subtask index of the sink and a rolling counter to determine the file names. For example with a\n74:  * prefix \"prefix\" and a suffix \".ext\", a file named {@code \"prefix-1-17.ext\"} contains the data\n75:  * from {@code subtask 1} of the sink and is the {@code 17th} bucket created by that subtask.\n76:  *\n77:  * <p>Part files roll based on the user-specified {@link RollingPolicy}. By default, a {@link\n78:  * DefaultRollingPolicy} is used for row-encoded sink output; a {@link OnCheckpointRollingPolicy} is\n79:  * used for bulk-encoded sink output.\n80:  *\n81:  * <p>In some scenarios, the open buckets are required to change based on time. In these cases, the\n82:  * user can specify a {@code bucketCheckInterval} (by default 1m) and the sink will check\n83:  * periodically and roll the part file if the specified rolling policy says so.\n84:  *\n85:  * <p>Part files can be in one of three states: {@code in-progress}, {@code pending} or {@code\n86:  * finished}. The reason for this is how the sink works together with the checkpointing mechanism to\n87:  * provide exactly-once semantics and fault-tolerance. The part file that is currently being written\n88:  * to is {@code in-progress}. Once a part file is closed for writing it becomes {@code pending}.\n89:  * When a checkpoint is successful the currently pending files will be moved to {@code finished}.\n90:  *\n91:  * <p>If case of a failure, and in order to guarantee exactly-once semantics, the sink should roll\n92:  * back to the state it had when that last successful checkpoint occurred. To this end, when\n93:  * restoring, the restored files in {@code pending} state are transferred into the {@code finished}\n94:  * state while any {@code in-progress} files are rolled back, so that they do not contain data that\n95:  * arrived after the checkpoint from which we restore.\n96:  *\n97:  * @param <IN> Type of the elements emitted by this sink\n98:  * @deprecated Use {@link org.apache.flink.connector.file.sink.FileSink} instead.\n99:  */\n100: @Internal\n101: public class StreamingFileSink<IN> extends RichSinkFunction<IN>\n102:         implements CheckpointedFunction, CheckpointListener {\n103: \n104:     private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n105: \n106:     // ------------------------ configuration fields --------------------------\n107: \n108:     private final long bucketCheckInterval;\n109: \n110:     private final BucketsBuilder<IN, ?, ? extends BucketsBuilder<IN, ?, ?>> bucketsBuilder;\n111: \n112:     // --------------------------- runtime fields -----------------------------\n113: \n114:     private transient StreamingFileSinkHelper<IN> helper;\n115: \n116:     /**\n117:      * Creates a new {@code StreamingFileSink} that writes files to the given base directory with\n118:      * the give buckets properties.\n119:      */\n120:     @VisibleForTesting\n121: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc@de39c3e1777c43fe3363b3fd7784bf46b57a99c2/-/blob/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/functions/sink/filesystem/legacy/StreamingFileSink.java%3FL1-120"}}}

It does that by implementing two phase commit algorithm on top of the\\n65:  * {@link CheckpointedFunction} and {@link CheckpointListener}. Use the new {@link\\n73:  *     org.apache.flink.api.connector.sink2.Sink} interface instead.\\n74:  */\\n75: @Internal\\n76: public abstract class TwoPhaseCommitSinkFunction<IN, TXN, CONTEXT> extends RichSinkFunction<IN>\\n77:         implements CheckpointedFunction, CheckpointListener {\\n78: \\n79:     private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TwoPhaseCommitSinkFunction.class);\\n80: \\n81:     protected final LinkedHashMap<Long, TransactionHolder<TXN>> pendingCommitTransactions =\\n82:             new LinkedHashMap<>();\\n83: \\n84:     protected transient Optional<CONTEXT> userContext;\\n85: \\n86:     protected transient ListState<State<TXN, CONTEXT>> state;\\n87: \\n88:     private final Clock clock;\\n89: \\n90:     private final ListStateDescriptor<State<TXN, CONTEXT>> stateDescriptor;\\n91: \\n92:     /**\\n93:      * Current Transaction Holder, including two states: 1.
